1. During intraoral examination the dentist suspected that the patient has syphilis. What should the dentist do in this case?
*a. Complete the examination and refer the patient for necessary tests
b. Inform the patient of the suspected diagnosis and end the visit
c. Obtain the impressions to study the diagnostic models
d. Continue the examination and start the teeth preparation
e. Decline to provide dental services for this patient

2. According to the professional standards, a dental orthopedist with work experience of 7 years and 6 months received qualification category I. How long must be the dentist's record of service, to be eligible for the next certification?
a. 9 years
b. 8 years
*c. 10 years
d. 12 years
e. 15 years

3. A man came to a dentist with complaints of a painless tumor-like formation on his left lower jaw. Palpation detects Dupuytren's sign. The crown of tooth 36 has a deep carious cavity. In the area of the rooth apices of tooth 36, X-ray shows an area of bone destruction 2x2 cm in size with clear margins. What is the most likely diagnosis in this case?
a. Giant-cell tumor of bone
b. Follicular cyst of the lower jaw
c. Mandibular keratocyst
d. Mandibular ameloblastoma
*e. Radicular cyst of the lower jaw

4. A 38-year-old man, an arc welder, is a chain smoker. He came to the dentist to have a denture made for him. Howerver, in the middle of his lower lip against the background of unchanged vermillion border there is a gray-white polygonal lesion 6x4 mm with clear margins. The lesion is covered with tightly attached small scales and is level with the vermillion border (neither protruding nor retracted). Palpation of the lesion focus is painless, the lesion has no thickened base; lateral palpation detects thickened surface of the lesion. Regional lymph nodes are unchanged. Make the provisional diagnosis:
a. Verrucous precancer
b. Lichen ruber planus, hyperkeratotic form
*c. Localized precancerous hyperkeratosis
d. Cancer of the lower lip
e. Lupus erythematosus

5. A 6-year-old boy with congenital heart disease (pulmonary artery stenosis) presents with suppurative periostitis of the maxilla. The child needs surgical treatment. What unit should he be referred to?
a. The out-patient unit, no precautions are necessary
*b. The pediatric maxillofacial unit
c. The out-patient or in-patient unit at the discretion of the child's parents
d. The cardiology unit
e. The out-patient unit after preliminary cardiological treatment

6. A removable complete denture is being made for the lower jaw of a 50-year-old man. During the fitting of an individual impression tray, the border in the area of the mylohyoid line needs to be determined. What Herbst test should be performed for this purpose?
a. Stretching the tongue towards the tip of the nose
*b. Licking the upper lip
c. Swallowing saliva
d. Wide mouth opening
e. Alternately touching the right and left cheeks with the tongue

7. A 27-year-old man presents with missing crown of 11. Objectively teeth 21 and 12 are intact; intraoral spot film X-ray shows the root of 11 to be filled to the apex, no changes in the periapical tissues, no pathologic mobility. What construction of the denture should be recommended for this patient?
a. Stump inlay with overlaying full cast metal crown
*b. Metal stump inlay with overlaying porcelain-fused-to-metal crown
c. Stump inlay with overlaying swaged crown
d. Stump inlay with overlaying plastic crown
e. Remove the root of 11 and perform implantation

8. Removable partial dentures for both jaws are being made for a 70-year-old man. To make diagnostic models, alginate impressions of both jaws need to be obtained. To prepare the alginate mass, the doctor mixes the powder with water in a rubber flask. Within what interval should the doctor apply the impression mass to the tray and place the tray in the patient's oral cavity?
a. Over 10 minutes
b. 5-10 minutes
*c. 3-5 minutes
d. Less than 3 minutes
e. Less than 1 minute

9. A 20-year-old woman complains of pain in the area of tooth 38. The pain increases during swallowing and opening her mouth wide. Objectively, the crown of tooth 38 is partially covered in mucosa, from under which a purulent exudate is being discharged. Palpation is painful. The mucosa over tooth 38 is hyperemic and swollen. a. Acute suppurative periostitis
b. Acute catarrhal pericoronitis
*c. Acute suppurative pericoronitis
d. Acute serous periostitis
e. Acute ulcerative pericoronitis

10. A 43-year-old man complains of a periodic feeling of heaviness in his right buccal region and a salty taste in his mouth with frequent exacerbations. Objectively, his parotid salivary gland on the right is dense, elastic, springy, and painless. Thick saliva with translucent mucus inclusions is being secreted from the duct opening. The sialogram revealed numerous small cavities in the parenchyma of the gland. What is the most likely diagnosis in this case?
a. Sjogren's syndrome
b. Chronic interstitial parotitis
*c. Chronic parenchymal parotitis
d. Pleomorphic adenoma of the parotid gland
e. Herzenberg's parotitis

11. A 5-year-old girl has a round soft elastic neoplasm up to 2 cm in diameter on the front surface of her neck on the midline. *a. Midline cervical cyst
b. Cervical dermoid cyst
c. Cyst of a submandibular salivary gland
d. Chronic hyperplastic lymphadenitis
e. Retention cyst of a sublingual salivary gland

12. A 28-year-old woman complains of a cavity in her lower left lateral tooth. Objective examination detects a mesio-occlusal-distal (MOD) defect of hard tissues of tooth 36. d. Model casting

13. A 22-year-old woman came to a dentist for preventive examination of her oral cavity. 14. A 45-year-old man after a tooth extraction carried out by a dentist complained of sudden weakness and intense bursting retrosternal pain that radiated under the left shoulder blade. 18.
